# ðŸ§  LeetCode Algorithm Quiz App

A Next.js application that helps you master algorithm identification by showing LeetCode problems and challenging you to select which algorithms can solve them.

## ðŸš€ Features

- **Interactive Quiz Interface**: Choose between Practice Mode and Timed Challenge
- **3,662 Real LeetCode Problems**: All current LeetCode problems with accurate data
- **44 Algorithm Types**: Comprehensive coverage of all algorithm categories
- **Smart Scoring System**: F1-score based evaluation for precise and comprehensive answers
- **Multiple Difficulty Levels**: Easy (892), Medium (1,907), Hard (863) problems
- **Real-time Timer**: Challenge yourself in timed mode
- **Detailed Feedback**: Learn which algorithms are correct after each submission
- **80% Free Problems**: 2,932 free problems, 730 premium problems

## ðŸŽ¯ Quiz Modes

### Practice Mode
- 5 random problems
- Unlimited time
- Detailed explanations
- Perfect for learning

### Timed Challenge  
- 10 random problems
- Race against the clock
- Competitive scoring
- Test your expertise

## ðŸ›  Algorithm Types Covered

- **Two Pointers** - Efficient array/string traversal
- **Sliding Window** - Substring and subarray problems
- **Binary Search** - Logarithmic search in sorted data
- **Hash Table** - Fast lookups and frequency counting
- **Dynamic Programming** - Optimization problems
- **Greedy** - Local optimum choices
- **Backtracking** - Exhaustive search with pruning
- **Depth-First Search (DFS)** - Tree and graph traversal
- **Breadth-First Search (BFS)** - Level-order traversal
- **Union Find** - Disjoint set operations
- **Heap/Priority Queue** - Maintain sorted order
- **Stack** - LIFO data structure problems
- **Queue** - FIFO data structure problems
- **Linked List** - Pointer manipulation
- **Tree Traversal** - Binary tree operations
- **Graph** - Network and connectivity problems
- **Trie** - Prefix tree for string problems
- **Bit Manipulation** - Bitwise operations
- **Math** - Mathematical computations
- **Sorting** - Ordering elements
- **Divide and Conquer** - Problem decomposition
- **Monotonic Stack** - Maintaining order invariant
- **Prefix Sum** - Cumulative calculations
- **Binary Indexed Tree** - Range queries
- **Segment Tree** - Range operations

## ðŸŽ® Getting Started

1. **Clone the repository**
```bash
git clone <repository-url>
cd speedcoders
```

2. **Install dependencies**
```bash
npm install
```

3. **Run the development server**
```bash
npm run dev
```

4. **Open your browser**
Navigate to [http://localhost:3000/quiz](http://localhost:3000/quiz) to start the quiz!

## ðŸŽ¯ How It Works

1. **Choose Your Mode**: Select Practice or Timed Challenge
2. **Pick Difficulty**: Easy, Medium, Hard, or Mixed problems
3. **Read the Problem**: Understand the LeetCode problem statement
4. **Select Algorithms**: Choose all algorithms that can solve the problem
5. **Submit & Learn**: Get instant feedback with correct algorithms highlighted
6. **Track Progress**: See your score and improvement over time

## ðŸ† Scoring System

The quiz uses an F1-score based evaluation system:
- **Precision**: Accuracy of your selected algorithms
- **Recall**: How many correct algorithms you identified
- **F1-Score**: Harmonic mean of precision and recall
- **Points**: F1-Score Ã— 100 per question

## ðŸŽ¨ Modern UI Features

- **Gradient Backgrounds**: Beautiful color transitions
- **Smooth Animations**: Hover effects and transitions
- **Responsive Design**: Works on all screen sizes  
- **Loading States**: Skeleton loaders for better UX
- **Progress Tracking**: Visual progress bars
- **Color-Coded Feedback**: Green for correct, red for incorrect, yellow for missed

## ðŸ”— Links to LeetCode

Every problem includes a direct link to the original LeetCode problem page for further practice and discussion.

## ðŸš€ Tech Stack

- **Next.js 15** - React framework with App Router
- **TypeScript** - Type-safe development
- **Tailwind CSS** - Utility-first styling
- **Heroicons** - Beautiful icon set
